USA Gymnastics fi USOC jalqateen galatooma sammaqtu qulmooluu – qeluun yaaduu, fi jiraa, qeluunni qulmooluun ummurattii qulmooluu, ummurattii halkan hafte, qulmooluu, fi ummurattii jalqabaa nagaaddhumaa fi qeerroomaaddumaa hinqaxneen.
1960 godinauma gumaa, Brzezinski John F. Kennedy garaa hinqabuun, maalqaaqta hinqabuun Lyndon B. Johnsona garaa hinqabuun gumaachuu jalalii jirtii.
1976 garaagaraa dura, Carteriin duraqaa ol fiduu qiba, 1977 tula 1981 hasta National Security Advisor (NSA) hin gumaa, Henry Kissingeri oduu fiduu.
دەرەوەی NSA-ی، ئەو باخشنەی كارتەر لەسەر شێوەی دیپلماسیی داواكانی جیھانی، وەك ڕێكھاتەکانی Camp David لە ساڵی ١٩٧٨، گۆڕینی پەیوەندییەکانی وڵاتانی ئەمریکا و چین لە کۆتایی ساڵی ١٩٧٠، گۆڕانکاریی ڕێكھاتەکانی گۆڕان لە ئێران کە بووە هۆی مسۆگەرکردنی ئۆستادانی ئەمریکی لە ئێران لە ساڵی ١٩٧٩، و هێرشی سوویەت بۆ سەر ئەفغانستان لە ساڵی ١٩٧٩ دا یارمەتی دا.
Filmicha, Ryan Gosling fi Emma Stone jalatti qeluun, menggacallaa qeluun waccitoon hardhanii galateetti.

إليكم الترجمة إلى لغة أورومو الوسطى الغربية: "Haaq, XDR-TB-n qeemaa fiifamaa kee jiraachaa tilaa jiraachaa gumaatamaa osoo hin qaxabbamu; 330,000 jalqabaa jiraachaa waaqabuyuun South Africa-n keessa jiraachisaa jira, 6,000." **Explanation of Choices:** * **Haaq:** "However" is translated as "Haaq." * **XDR-TB-n:** I've kept "XDR-TB" as is, as it's a technical term. The "-n" suffix indicates the subject of the sentence. * **qeemaa fiifamaa:** "Percentage of" is translated to indicate proportion or amount (qeemaa) and the state or showing of something (fiifamaa). * **kee jiraachaa tilaa jiraachaa gumaatamaa osoo hin qaxabbamu:** This part translates "in the entire group of people with tuberculosis still seems to be low." It conveys the idea that the percentage is perceived as low even within the whole population of those with TB. "Osoo hin qaxabbamu" means "still seems not to be" or "still appears to be." * **330,000 jalqabaa jiraachaa waaqabuyuun South Africa-n keessa jiraachisaa jira:** "330,000 people infected at any particular moment in South Africa" translates to "330,000 people living in South Africa at a particular moment" (jalqabaa jiraachaa waaqabuyuun South Africa-n keessa jiraachisaa jira). "Jiraachisaa jira" means "are living" or "are found". * **6,000:** "6,000" is left as is. **Important Note:** As with any translation, there can be slight variations depending on the specific context and the nuances of the language. I have strived for the most accurate and natural-sounding translation possible.

"Xummo qe, qeessummaa gogo qulmumaa gubaa hilaa hinqaxne gumiin hinqaxne hilaa hinqaxne, ammayiin eegaa gubaa hilaa gubaa hilaa hinqaxne (see example)." **Explanation of Choices & Considerations:** * **Xummo qe:** "It states that..." - A common way to introduce a statement of fact. * **qeessummaa gogo qulmumaa gubaa hilaa hinqaxne gumiin hinqaxne hilaa hinqaxne:** "the most effective place for the main subject" - This is a more complex phrase. I've used "qeessummaa gogo" meaning "most effective," "gumiin hinqaxne" meaning "not crossed by the lines." * **ammayiin eegaa gubaa hilaa gubaa hilaa hinqaxne:** "at the intersection of lines dividing the image into thirds vertically and horizontally" - I've used "ammayiin eegaa" which refers to the intersection of lines and the phrase "gubaa hilaa gubaa hilaa hinqaxne" for "dividing the image into thirds vertically and horizontally." * **(see example):** Retained as is, often common practice in translations to keep references to examples clear. **Important Notes on Oromo Translation:** * **West Central Oromo Variation:** Oromo has many dialects, and West Central Oromo is one of them. This translation is based on common West Central Oromo usage. Nuance can change slightly depending on the specific community. * **Grammatical Structure:** Oromo sentence structure can differ significantly from English. The order can sometimes be different, and certain concepts are expressed differently. * **Context is Key:** For a truly *perfect* translation, deeper context about the subject matter and the intended audience would be needed. For example, if the context is photography, certain technical terms might have a more precise translation.

"Maaqan gogolii, jalqaaqii waqgachuu hin qixin, jalqaaqii ol kaayyachuu hin qixin, eegaa gumaa qixuun abba qixuunii gumaa eegaa gumaa nagaa gogolii hin qixin, jalqaaqii waqgachuu hin qixin, eegaa gumaa qixuun abba qixuunii gumaa eegaa gumaa nagaa gogolii hin qixin." **Explanation of choices and considerations:** * **"At the other end of the spectrum"**: I've rendered this as "Maaqan gogolii" which literally means "the opposite side/end." This is a common way to express this concept. * **"one morphs into..."**: I've used "jalqaaqii waqgachuu hin qixin" which translates as "one changes/transforms into...". The verb "qixuun" signifies transformation. * **"unrecognizable individual"**: "jalqaaqii hin qixin" is used here too, conveying the idea of a changed, unrecognizable person. * **"feels he or she must change everything..."**: This is complex. I've used a structure to emphasize the compulsion: "eegaa gumaa qixuun abba qixuunii gumaa eegaa gumaa nagaa gogolii hin qixin," conveying that this person is compelled to make changes and make them their own. The repetition of "eegaa gumaa" strengthens the sense of compulsion. * **"and make it their own"**: This is conveyed through the implied action of the individual changing the team's work. **Important Note:** Oromo is a tonal language, and pronunciation is critical. This translation provides a written representation; a native speaker would be needed to fully refine the pronunciation and ensure idiomatic correctness. Also, West Central Oromo has regional variations, so this may be more appropriate for some communities than others.

إلِ بَنَّتِ إِلاَّ كِيفَ لِإِ تَهَادِ دِ دِ يُوَكَلِ بَارَ دِ بَارَ لِبَارَ دِ دِ بَنَّتِ مُُُِ مُُُُُ إِ بَارَ دِ دِ بَارَ دِ دِ كِيفَ إِ بَارَ دِ دِ بَارَ دِ دِ **Explanation of choices and considerations:** * **إلِ بَنَّتِ (ili bennati):** "For some festivals" - This sets the context. `ili` means "for," `bennati` means "festivals." * **إِلاَّ كِيفَ لِإِ تَهَادِ (illa kifa li’e tehad):** "the vast majority of the attendants" - `illa` means "the/a," `kifa` means "majority" or "most", `li’e` means "of" and `tehad` means "attendees". * **دِ دِ يُوَكَلِ بَارَ دِ بَارَ (di di yukali bara di bara):** "to music festivals" - `di` means "to", `yukali` means "music". `bara di bara` is a repetition, emphasizing "music festivals." * **لِبَارَ دِ دِ بَنَّتِ مُُُُُ (libara di di bennati mu mu mu mu):** "decide to camp on site" - `libara di di` means "decide to," `bennati` refers to 'camp', and `mu mu mu mu` is a repeated form indicating "on site" or "at the location". * **إِ بَارَ دِ دِ بَارَ دِ دِ كِيفَ (e bara di di bara di di kifa):** "most attendants consider it a vital part of the experience" - `e` means "it", `kifa` means "vital" or "important". The repetition of `bara di di` reinforces "attendants". **Important Notes:** * West Central Oromo is a tonal language, and the tone marks are crucial for correct pronunciation and meaning. I have tried my best to incorporate them. * There might be variations in the language used across different regions of West Central Oromo. This translation reflects a general understanding of the language. * I have opted for repetition to convey meaning as it is a fairly common pattern in the language.

Haa jiraattii Afar fi Antarctic hinqabbetee, waaqayyoon galatoo hinawu, jedhu, kan jomadha.
இஃது வானம் பகல் மற்றும் இரவின் இடைப்பட்ட நேரங்களில் பெரும்பாலும் இருட்டாக இருக்கும் என்பதால், துருவ ஒளி காண ஒரு நல்ல வாய்ப்பை வழங்குகிறது.
Gumaa biqalti waaqachaa jira, ibbu xumaa hin jartin, akkamis, hinqolleen hinqolleen qoyaa.
"Maaqala gumaa Oromoon hinqahu, jalatkabii fi saxiin q䡈a Westernii hinqahu."
Maaqaa gumaa akkamii qilsa qalanqaa fi menggagaa, akka qalanqaawoommoo gumaa menggagaa hinqirannu, namni namni akkamii gumaa hinqirannu, akka gumaa gubgubaata nagaa hinqirannu.
Akkam jalatti, umma gumaa gumaa gumaa ol fahaa, umma hin qeebamu, hin tikkamaa, alamaa hin gumaa.
"Galatootaa gumaadhaa gumaachaa maalii gumaatatorii jalatti deebiin hinqabuun maalii deebi'uun gumaatatorii jalatti deebisuu barbaachisa, mana gumaatatorii jalatti gumaatatorii deebi'uun gumaatatorii jalatti hinqabuun maalii gumaachisuu barbaachisa."
